North and South portions have separate parking, connected by path & bridge crossing small stream. North portion is a large field with kids park and outdoor dining pavilion. < text>
I went to Tori's on a Friday nite around 9pm for the first time with friends. It's was okay considering...the hostess was M.I.A at the doorway. The place was packed with on-lookers in the front lounge/karaoke area hearing / watching in fright at the high pitched shrilling karaoke rendition of "phantom of the opera."

We would have waited forever if it wasn't for the smart thinking of my friend. We sat down and when the waitress asked us what we would like for drinks, I asked for cold sake. She didn't know if they had cold sake but knew they only carried two. Two? As wait staff new or old, you should know what's on hand.  I sushi chef knew what kind of cold sake the establishment had. We ordered the Nigiri, with shot glasses. We're going enjoy this night. Sad to say, the waitress came back and said they didn't have any more Nigiri, WTF! Really? For a Friday nite an establishment should be fully stocked to quench customer's who have had a ridiculously amazing week. So we just drank free tap water.

We ordered appetizers which took forever, so we ordered our sushi rolls. We were not in a hurry, but hungry. The sushi chef did double duty being sushi maker and waitress since we didn't have chopsticks or napkins. We ordered our appetizers which came late, after we went through our sushi rolls. The sushi rolls were good like any other place. The only thing was they fell apart easily.

Overall, if you want karaoke, sushi, Teppanyaki , and spotty service, Tori's is the place for you.

There are other sushi places in Modesto with less noise, comparable prices, sushi and better service.<//text>

<name>Ashley< /name><Time>1512367206878< /Time>< rating>
2< /rating>
<Review>I had been going here for about 4 years. If I had written this review 3 years into my regular visits, I would have given it 4 stars--tasty food but mediocre service.

So why the demotion to 2 stars?

This is my experience the last three times I've ordered takeout (I gave it the benefit of the doubt, but now I'm done):

1. Ordered a tofu curry. Got home and realized that they had given me the beef version of the curry. Had to drive back to get my proper order. Nothing comped for my troubles.

2. Ordered the same tofu curry. Checked that it was correct. Got home and on the last bite, bit into a chunk of...pork? chicken? Something definitely NOT tofu.

3. Ordered my usual tofu curry. Get home. Realize that there are small bits of shredded meat throughout my dish.

Sigh. Luckily, my tofu-love is not the result of a severe dietary restriction or rigid moral positions, but it was still incredibly distasteful to have meat in what was meant to be a meat-free dish.

I don't know what happened--a cook change? Lax quality control?--but after three times in a row, I just cannot justify going back, and this had been my favorite Thai place in town.

It has been a while since this experience, so hopefully they have fixed this issue, but I was severely disappointed with these problems and have not been back since.< /Review><pics>None</pics>< response>
None</response>

< Text>
This spot is one of two Thai restaurants in Vallejo. It's good, to be sure, but when you've eaten at other Thai restaurants in the bay, it's not anything that's all that special in particular.

First and foremost, this place is probably one of the better spots in Vallejo if you're craving something that's in the realm of ethnic cuisine. The decor and overall environs of the restaurant are nice and clean. Almost a tropical feel to this place. Energy and vibe are great too. Some Friday nights, there's even local live music which is really nice. Staff here are consistently friend and helpful. Service is always fast, even when it's packed.

Now, the food itself. I've ordered the majority of the stuff on the menu within the 12 year span that I've been frequenting this place. Curries, pad thai, spicy dishes, grilled meats, and the seafoods. All of it? Good food and by no means bad at all. But having since also visited other Thai restaurants, I will say that the food here is not spectacular. But again, the food here is not bad at all. If you're local and not looking to set foot outside of the city, I would recommend this place (though Ano Thai Lao might be a better choice, depending on your location in the city.) This place is OK overall.</Text>

I explained to him that the appointment was made before the manufacturer's warranty had run out and that the square trade warranty covered it now.  I then called Costco Concierge Services who called them, only to get a call 3 HOURS LATER from the manager at Paradise to tell me that they would not be coming out and that I should call another company to fix my dishwasher.  I would suggest that anyone who needs their appliance fixed goes with another company as this one gives you at best a 25% shot of them even coming out.
